ESCALATE VERB AUTHORIZATION (pkg/registry/rbac/escalation_check.go):\\n   - RoleEscalationAuthorized() checks if a user has explicit 'escalate' permission on roles/clusterroles resources. BINDING AUTHORIZATION (pkg/registry/rbac/escalation_check.go):\\n   - BindingAuthorized() checks if a user has explicit 'bind' permission on role/clusterrole resources, used for RoleBinding/ClusterRoleBinding creation.\\n\\n3. This function constructs an authorization request with Verb='escalate' and checks it against the RBAC authorizer.\\n   - EscalationAllowed() checks if the user is in the system:masters group, which bypasses escalation checks.\\n   - The 'escalate' verb is used to determine if a user can modify Role/ClusterRole objects without role escalation restrictions.\\n\\n2. BINDING AUTHORIZATION (pkg/registry/rbac/escalation_check.go):\\n   - BindingAuthorized() checks if a user has explicit 'bind' permission on role/clusterrole resources, used for RoleBinding/ClusterRoleBinding creation.\\n\\n3. RULE COVERAGE VALIDATION (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go):\\n   - ConfirmNoEscalation() validates that the rules a user is trying to grant are already covered by rules the user possesses.\\n   - This is enforced by retrieving the user's current rules via ruleResolver.RulesFor() and comparing them against the new rules using validation.Covers().\\n   - If the user's rules do not cover the new rules being granted, the operation is forbidden.\\n\\n4. RULE COMPARISON LOGIC (staging/src/k8s.io/component-helpers/auth/rbac/validation/policy_comparator.go):\\n   - Covers() compares owner rules against servant rules by breaking them down into atomic components.\\n   - BreakdownRule() decomposes a PolicyRule into individual subrules, one for each combination of verb, resource, and resource name.\\n   - ruleCovers() performs the actual rule matching, comparing verbs using VerbMatches() and other attributes.\\n\\n5. ENFORCEMENT POINTS:\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrole/policybased/storage.go: Enforces escalation checks during ClusterRole Create/Update operations. Also checks for aggregation rules which require cluster-admin.\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/role/policybased/storage.go: Enforces escalation checks for Role objects using RoleEscalationAuthorized().\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrolebinding/policybased/storage.go: Enforces binding authorization and rule coverage checks.\\n   - pkg/registry/rbac/rolebinding/policybased/storage.go: Enforces binding authorization and rule coverage checks for namespaced bindings.\\n\\n6. VERB MATCHING (pkg/apis/rbac/v1/evaluation_helpers.go):\\n   - VerbMatches() checks if a policy rule's verbs include the requested verb or the wildcard '*' verb.\\n   - The function is used throughout the authorization chain to verify verb permissions.\\n\\nThe escalation prevention system prevents a user from creating or modifying roles/rolebindings to grant themselves permissions they do not currently hold, effectively closing privilege escalation paths. The 'escalate' verb provides a way for administrators to explicitly grant users the ability to modify roles without these restrictions, while the 'bind' verb controls binding permissions separately.\"\n}\n","numLines":197,"startLine":1,"totalLines":197}}}
